 Savita means Surya or Tej, but it is not so with reference to poetess Savita Singh
 apane naam ke saath singh lagane ke baad bhi vah keval 'stri' he

 bihar ke aara jile ke sampann parivaar main 5 farvari, 1962 unka janm hua
 The language of instruction was English and the home language was Bhojpuri, Hindi
 mata-pita desh ke baahar rahete the, so har chuttee main unase milane videsh janaa or padhai ke dinon main khub padhanaa unke liye shagal jaisaa tha

 dilli vishvavidhyalay se eme, emphil karne ke baad ucch shiksha ke liye vah motrial ke macgil vishvavidhyalay chali gayi

 vah chaar saal canada or do saal landan main raheen

 bharat lautin to adhyaapan se jud gayi

 unki rachanaatmak uplabdhiyaan academik uplabdhiyon jaisi hi baribharakam hai

 samakaleen vaicharik muddon sahit antarrashtriya patr-patrikaon main unke shodh-patr tathaa saahitiyik rachanaaen chhapati rahi hai
 His first collection of poems 'apne Jaise Jeevan' was awarded by the Hindi Academy in 2001
 unhone stri ke marm ko itani shiddat se mahasusa ki unki kavitaaon main vah apane aap abhivyakt hote gaye
 Its hallmark is found in most of his poems
 par savita singh ke kavita kii stri keval dard kii hi nahin, saahas kii bhi pratimurti he

 ' yah saal 2005 main chapa

 saal 2011 main unhone america, europe or asia kii saat kavyitriyon ke angrezi sankalan 'seven leeves, van autom' kaa sampadan kiya
 In 2012, his representative poems were printed under the name 'for the new century: fifty poems'
 unka teesraa kavita sankalan 'swapn samay' ke naam se chapa

 jisamen har roj nai chijen sikhti thi, nai chijen padhati thi, nae logon se milti thi, nae fal khaati thi

 haalanki mere mata-pita hameshaa videsh main rahete the
 We got good Indian education so they had left us here
 yahaan ham ek sanyukt, bharepure parivaar main chachaa, chachee, dada-daadi, bhai-bahan sabhi ke saath rahete the

 par mata-pita ke saath na rahane kaa asar manovaigyanik rup se rahata tha

 shaayad isiilie maine apana puraa samay padhane-likhane main laga diya

 vah aapke swa kaa hissaa he

 isiilie maine apane ko gyaan arjeet karne main laga diya

 isse maine logon se cat kar apana ek alag ekant bana liya

 in vidhayakon ko raajbahadur ke netritv main basapa vidrohi gut main shaamil hone ke liye or ek kaagaj par mulaayam singh sarkaar ko samarthan dene kii shapath lete hue dastakhat karne ko kaha gaya tha
 Some of them were so scared that they signed it on blank paper
 vidhayakon ko raat main kaaphi der tak vahaan bandi banaae rakhaa gaya, jis samay atithigrih main basapa vidhayakon ko is tarah se dhar kar dabocha ja rahaa tha, jaise murgiyon ko kasaai khaane le jaaya ja rahaa ho, kamaron ke set 1-2 ke saamne, jahaan mayawati kuch vidhayakon ke saath baithi thim
 a strange drama was happening, some mlas escaped from the crowd outside and took refuge to hide in the same rooms
 andar aane vaale aakhri varisht basapa netaa aarake choudhary the, jinhen sipaahi rashid ahamed or choudhary ke nijee rakshak lalchand kii dekharekh main bachaa kar laae the
 The mlas hiding in the rooms were instructed by Lalchand to lock the doors from inside and they had just closed the doors so that a mob from the crowd roamed the corridor and started banging the door
 mayawati ko do kanishtha police afasaron himmat ne bachaaya
 These were Vijay Bhushan, the House Officer (SHO) at Hazratganj station, and Subhash Singh Baghel, who was the SHO (VIP), who took some of the soldiers along and pushed back the crowd with great difficulty
 phir ve sab galiyare main kataribaddh hokar khadey ho gaye taaki koi bhi unhen paar na kar sake
 The angry mob still kept shouting slogans and abusing and threatened to drag Mayawati out
 kuch police afasaron kii is sahaspurn or samayik kaarywahi ke alaava, zyaadaatar upasthit adhikariyon ne jinamein rajya atithi grih main sanchaalak or suraksha karmchaaree bhi shaamil the, is puure paagalpan ko rokane kii koi koshish nahin kii
 This all went on for over an hour
 kai basapa vidhayakon or kuch police adhikariyon ke ye bayaan stambhit karne vaale the ki jab vidhayakon ko apharan kiya ja rahaa tha or mayawati ke kamaron ke akraman ho rahaa tha, us samay vahaan lakhanu ke senior suprintedent of police opi singh bhi maujuud the
 According to eyewitnesses, they were just standing and blowing cigarettes
 akraman shuru hone ke turant baad rahasyatmak dhang se, atithi grih kii bijli or pani kii supplai kaat di gai-prashasan kii mileebhagat kaa ek or sanket
 The situation there improved only after the District Magistrate of Lucknow arrived there
 unhone krodhit bheed kaa dat kar muqabla karne kii himmat or jaagrukta kaa parichay diya
 The District Magistrate, together with SP Rajiv Ranjan, first pushed the members of the mob outside the confines of the guest house, who were not mlas
 baad main police ke atirikt bal sanghathanon ke aane par unhone sapa ke vidhayakon samet sabhi ko rajya atithi-grih ke daayre ke baahar nikalava diya
 However, to do so, he had to resort to the lathi charge of the mlas
 phir bhi sapa ke vidhansabha sadasyon ke khilaaf kaarywahi na karne kii mukhyamantri ke karyaalay se mili chetavanee ko ansuni karke ve apane faisle par date rahe
 The transfer order was issued to the District Magistrate with immediate effect after 11 o'clock at night, as a result of not doing his duty without fear and favor
 tippaniyan As more and more defense teams started reaching the Governor's office, the central government and senior BJP leaders interfered, the situation inside the guest house was controlled
 jab rakshakon ne building ke andar or baahar kabja kar liya tab gaaliyaan, dhamkiyaan or naare lagaati hui bheed dhire-dhire kam hoti chali gai
 Mayawati and her group of party mlas who had locked themselves inside the room set 1-2, had to make repeated requests to the District Magistrate and other officials to make sure that the threat was averted, and they opened the door
 Could jab unhone darwaja kholaa, tab tak kaaphi raat ho chuki thi
 Since then, Mayawati and Mulayam Singh's relationship deteriorated
 uske baad se 24 saal tak donon dalon ke bich naa to chunaav purv or naa hi chunaav ke baad koi gathbandhan hua he
 It remains to be seen whether the hostility caused by the guest house scandal in the SP-BSP changes
 kaha jaataa he ki jab gundon ne baad main brahmadatt dvivedi kii goli markar hatya kar di tab mayawati unke ghar gayi or foot-foot kar royee
 When her widow contested the election, Mayawati did not field any candidate against her, but appealed to the people to vote for my brother's widow who was martyred by taking hostility to save my life
 kuch reporton ke anusaar cheekh-pukaar machaate hue ve (samaajawaadee party ke vidhayak, kaaryakarta or bheed) ashleel bhashaa or gaali-galouj kaa istemaal kar rahe the
 The mlas sitting in the Common Hall (bahujan Samaj Party mlas) quickly closed the main gate, but the herd broke it open
 phir ve asahaay basapa vidhayakon par tut pade or unhen thappad maarane or latiyaane lage
 It is said that at least five BSP mlas were dragged and forced into vehicles on the outside of the guest house which took them to the Chief Minister's residence
 in vidhayakon ko raajbahadur ke netritv main basapa vidrohi gut main shaamil hone ke liye or ek kaagaj par mulaayam singh sarkaar ko samarthan dene kii shapath lete hue dastakhat karne ko kaha gaya tha
 Some of them were so scared that they signed it on blank paper
 vidhayakon ko raat main kaaphi der tak vahaan bandi banaae rakhaa gaya, jis samay atithigrih main basapa vidhayakon ko is tarah se dhar kar dabocha ja rahaa tha, jaise murgiyon ko kasaai khaane le jaaya ja rahaa ho, kamaron ke set 1-2 ke saamne, jahaan mayawati kuch vidhayakon ke saath baithi thim
 a strange drama was happening, some mlas escaped from the crowd outside and took refuge to hide in the same rooms
 andar aane vaale aakhri varisht basapa netaa aarake choudhary the, jinhen sipaahi rashid ahamed or choudhary ke nijee rakshak lalchand kii dekharekh main bachaa kar laae the
 The mlas hiding in the rooms were instructed by Lalchand to lock the doors from inside and they had just closed the doors so that a mob from the crowd roamed the corridor and started banging the door
 mayawati ko do kanishtha police afasaron himmat ne bachaaya
 These were Vijay Bhushan, the House Officer (SHO) at Hazratganj station, and Subhash Singh Baghel, who was the SHO (VIP), who took some of the soldiers along and pushed back the crowd with great difficulty
 phir ve sab galiyare main kataribaddh hokar khadey ho gaye taaki koi bhi unhen paar na kar sake
 The angry mob still kept shouting slogans and abusing and threatened to drag Mayawati out
 kuch police afasaron kii is sahaspurn or samayik kaarywahi ke alaava, zyaadaatar upasthit adhikariyon ne jinamein rajya atithi grih main sanchaalak or suraksha karmchaaree bhi shaamil the, is puure paagalpan ko rokane kii koi koshish nahin kii
 This all went on for over an hour
 kai basapa vidhayakon or kuch police adhikariyon ke ye bayaan stambhit karne vaale the ki jab vidhayakon ko apharan kiya ja rahaa tha or mayawati ke kamaron ke akraman ho rahaa tha, us samay vahaan lakhanu ke senior suprintedent of police opi singh bhi maujuud the
 According to eyewitnesses, they were just standing and blowing cigarettes
 akraman shuru hone ke turant baad rahasyatmak dhang se, atithi grih kii bijli or pani kii supplai kaat di gai-prashasan kii mileebhagat kaa ek or sanket
 The situation there improved only after the District Magistrate of Lucknow arrived there
 unhone krodhit bheed kaa dat kar muqabla karne kii himmat or jaagrukta kaa parichay diya
 The District Magistrate, together with SP Rajiv Ranjan, first pushed the members of the mob outside the confines of the guest house, who were not mlas
 baad main police ke atirikt bal sanghathanon ke aane par unhone sapa ke vidhayakon samet sabhi ko rajya atithi-grih ke daayre ke baahar nikalava diya
 However, to do so, he had to resort to the lathi charge of the mlas
 phir bhi sapa ke vidhansabha sadasyon ke khilaaf kaarywahi na karne kii mukhyamantri ke karyaalay se mili chetavanee ko ansuni karke ve apane faisle par date rahe
 The transfer order was issued to the District Magistrate with immediate effect after 11 o'clock at night, as a result of not doing his duty without fear and favor
 tippaniyan As more and more defense teams started reaching the Governor's office, the central government and senior BJP leaders interfered, the situation inside the guest house was controlled
 jab rakshakon ne building ke andar or baahar kabja kar liya tab gaaliyaan, dhamkiyaan or naare lagaati hui bheed dhire-dhire kam hoti chali gai
 Mayawati and her group of party mlas who had locked themselves inside the room set 1-2, had to make repeated requests to the District Magistrate and other officials to make sure that the threat was averted, and they opened the door

 - input bhashaa Like religion, patriotism is a personal expression that is expressed in a very intimate way and that is why it has different meanings for different people like religion

 hota he

 What the movies talk about has a lot of connection with the era in which they are made

 His pride is a manifestation of the human spirit
 unki uplabdhi kisi tuchh or naganya samajhe jane vaale ko chamakane kaa mauka milane kii he
 For me Lagaan was not just a film showing patriotism
 yah logon ke saahas kii katha thi
 When i started working on Raazi (2018), i never thought that i was making any patriotic film while going through the processes of writing, cinematography, production and editing
 mere liye yah film durdamaneey maanviya bhaavana, dridhtaa, or yuddh kii nirarthakta kii kahani thi

 agar aap dhyaan den to aapako raji main kahin bhi bhartiya jhanda nahin dikhegaa

 meraa iraadaa sachhee dridhtaa kii ek kahani dikhaane kaa tha
 i did not want to teach patriotic lessons with this
 iske mukhya charitra sahamat (aalia bhatta) kii ore jis baat ne mujhe khinchaa tha vah yah thi ki us jaisaa bhi koi kabhi is duniya main maujuud tha
 i think this character was a role model, an inspiration
 use dekhte hue aapmen gahare santosh or unnayan kaa bhav paidaa ho saktaa he

 yah sanyog bhar he ki jab logon ne film ko dekhnaa shuru kiya or samikshakon ne samikshaayen likhni shuru kin to ham jin arthon ke saath ise le kar chale the, usase aage ke arth bhi khulne lage
 It emerged as a film that portrayed Desh Prem from a different perspective
 isamen dekha ja saktaa tha ki ugr rashtravaadi abhivyaktiyon kaa sahaara liye bina bhi aap deshbhakti ho sakate hai
 When we were writing the characters of the Pakistani family of Sehmat, we might have unknowingly made sure that their behavior, actions and decisions were not governed by nationalist influence
 isiilie jab aap in pakistani charitron ke saamne rakh kar sahamat ko dekhte hai to vah aapako khalanayika lagati he

 lekin jaise hi aap un vajahon kaa khyaal karte hai jinke chalate vah aisa kar rahi he to achaanak uske prati bhaavon kii nakaaratmakataa khatm ho jaati he
 As soon as the factors that motivate her are removed, she again seems to be the antagonist, not her Pakistani family
 'shatru paksh' ko maanviya banaae rakhte hue sahamat ko naitik rup se thik sabit kiye rakhana apane aap main chunauti thi
 This balance could have deteriorated a little when leaning towards anything
 bhavukta mujhe bahut pareshaan nahin karti, lekin jab dambh kisi bhaavana ke rup main phere lagane lagaataa he to mere bheetar kii ghanti baj jaati he
 If i am portraying the patriotism of Sehmat in the film, i should also speak about her husband Iqbal's love for her country
 ek kii deshbhakti duusare kii keemat par kyon ho? agar hamaare saath hamaara deshprem he, to hamen dusron ke deshprem ko bhi sweekaar karnaa chahie
 According to me, i do not have to hate any other country to love my country
 ant main, iraadaa hi vah cheez he jo sabase zyada mahatvapurn hota he
 When we made Talwar (2015), we did not want to get into any controversy
 ham keval kahani ke donon pakshon ko saamne laana chaahate the kyonki hamen lag rahaa tha ki is bare main jo samachar hamaare bich aae the ve asantulit the
 We had no solution
 ham keval sari jaankaree saamne rakhana chaahate the
 This is your intention, which i think is visible to everyone
 is lihaaj se deshbhakti kaa chithran bhi bilkul aisi hi baat he
 Whatever my portrayals of patriotism, my intentions have an impact on them
 mere liye mere desh kaa arth he mere log, meraa shahar or meraa vaataavaran
 It is certainly not an ideology
 apane desh ke prati prem vyakt karne ke liye mujhe apane chehre par tirangaa banavaane kii jarurat nahin he
 i believe that if i immerse myself in my work, then i can bring out a little something that can help improve this nation
 main jhanda fahraane yaa naare lagane kaa kaam nahin kar sakati
 i should not have to prove my patriotism in my films or in my life
 mujhe aisa karne ke liye kaha bhi nahin janaa chahie

 dilli kii hawa lagaataar jahrili hoti ja rahi he
 On the one hand, while there is a feeling of change in the weather, in the states like Haryana and Punjab, pollution has increased in the capital after burning of stubble
 gauratlab he ki adhikariyon ne aane vaale dinon main halaat bigadane kii chetavanee di he
 In such a situation, some students from IIT Delhi have found an eco-friendly solution to this problem
 isse naa keval paraali jalaane ko roka ja sakegaa, balki kisaanon ko rice straw kii acchhee keemat milegi or plastic kii jagah paper kii chizon kaa istemaal kiya ja sakegaa
 In fact, Ankur, Kanika and Prachar, who were out of the iits last year, have designed a machine to convert rice straw into pulp
 phir isi pulp ko plates or anya iko-friendli teblevair banane ke liye istemaal kiya ja saktaa he
 The steps are as follows
 
 
 > pehle paraali ko chote-chote tukdon main ek mashin ke jariye kaata jaataa he
 > Then this parali is washed in the washing machine of the house and dried with the help of a drainer
 yah step paraali kii gandagi ko nikaalane ke liye hota he
 > After this, the straw is added to the digester using eco-friendly or green chemicals
 > digester se nikali paraali behad mulaayam hoti he, jise beter main kuch ek ghante ke liye beet kiya jaataa he
 > After which the final pulp is prepared
 ek do chote-mote or steps ke baad is pulp ko teblevair companyj ke paas bheja jaataa he jo isse bio-degradable chijen banaati hai
 For such things, IIT students have made slogan 'eat-throw'
 students kaa kahana he ki is mashin ke jariye kisaan kareeb 5000 rupye prati acre bana paaenge
 This will be very beneficial for the farmers as they have been complaining that rice is not a market for straw
 2 se 3 mahino main students kaa daawa he ki is mashin ko market main utaara ja sakegaa
 a machine that will prevent the use of plastic along with burning stubble
